Dropdown - " data-et-label="Why buy a domain name from Namecheap?" data-et-customhandler=homePage.faqDropdown> <span class="gb-text-large gb-text-bold">Why buy a domain name from Namecheap?</span> </div>   <div class="gb-collapse__content gb-pl-3"> <p>Above all else, we strive to deliver outstanding customer experiences. When you buy a domain name from Namecheap, we guarantee it will be handed over to you with superior standards of service and support. Our primary goal is to build a customer-focused atmosphere filled with the happiest customers in the galaxy. The Namecheap guarantee is our mark of excellence.</p> </div>  </div>  <div class=gb-collapse>  <div class=gb-collapse__trigger data-et-category="New homepage" data-et-action="FAQ - Dropdown - " data-et-label="Why is domain name registration required?" data-et-customhandler=homePage.faqDropdown> <span class="gb-text-large gb-text-bold">Why is domain name registration required?</span> </div>   <div class="gb-collapse__content gb-pl-3"> <p>When you build a website, you want visitors to come and see what you've done. To get them there, you need a unique domain name that connects to your site's servers. Domain name registration is required to ensure that no one else in the world can claim ownership of your site's address and to make finding your website simple. <a href="https://www.namecheap.com/domains/domain-name-search/" data-et-category="New homepage" data-et-action="FAQ - Dropdown - Link" data-et-label="/domains/domain-name-search/">Find your one of a kind domain name.</a></p> </div>  </div>  <div class=gb-collapse>  <div class=gb-collapse__trigger data-et-category="New homepage" data-et-action="FAQ - Dropdown - " data-et-label="How does domain registration work?" data-et-customhandler=homePage.faqDropdown> <span class="gb-text-large gb-text-bold">How does domain registration work?</span> </div>   <div class="gb-collapse__content gb-pl-3"> <p>Think of the name you want to register. The answer is typically your company or website name. It is best to keep your domain name short and easy to understand. Say it out loud, and make sure it sounds great. Next, search to see if it is available. If the name you desire is taken with the .com top-level domain, there are hundreds of others available. Finally, add the top choices to your cart and complete the domain registration.</p> </div>  </div>  <div class=gb-collapse>  <div class=gb-collapse__trigger data-et-category="New homepage" data-et-action="FAQ - Dropdown - " data-et-label="What domains are available from Namecheap?" data-et-customhandler=homePage.faqDropdown> <span class="gb-text-large gb-text-bold">What domains are available from Namecheap?</span> </div>   <div class="gb-collapse__content gb-pl-3"> <p>At Namecheap, you can register brand new domain names using hundreds of popular TLDs. All of which come as standard with Namecheap — alongside a great price, of course.</p> </div>  </div>  <div class=gb-collapse>  <div class=gb-collapse__trigger data-et-category="New homepage" data-et-action="FAQ - Dropdown - " data-et-label="How do I pick the right domain name?" data-et-customhandler=homePage.faqDropdown> <span class="gb-text-large gb-text-bold">How do I pick the right domain name?</span> </div>   <div class="gb-collapse__content gb-pl-3"> <p>So you’ve discovered that simply Googling ‘register website domain’ and finding a great provider isn’t the whole story.
